# ETRM System — Project Handoff Document
**Version:** 2.22 | **Date:** July 2026 | **Status:** Trade Capture + Credit & Risk Module Complete — migration frontier V126 (`dbo.book_ownership` — book-level JV/economic participation, independent of the parent legal entity's own ownership/type; shares a new `components/smart/OwnershipPanel.tsx` with V125's entity-level `dbo.legal_entity_ownership`); closed the "17 endpoints missing `@Valid`" pending item (real NPE fixes, not just message-quality — see 2026-07-19 §0 entries) (`dbo.legal_entity_ownership` — Joint Venture cap-table sub-resource: polymorphic owner (legal entity/counterparty/external), operator flag, consolidation method, new Ownership tab on the Legal Entity drawer); `BookTreeExplorer` recursive hierarchy UI with create/edit + roll-up P&L + "Book Manager" sidebar group; full-app backend build in progress (Master Data modules); Voyage & Charter Ops (Time Charter / Bunker / Laytime backbone) + Maritime Execution Platform phase 2 (Fleet, Vessel Performance, Charter Party Templates, Port Activity Templates, Cargo Tank/Hold Config, Emission Factors, Operational Status/Delay Codes) + vessel_type FK conversion + payment_term/unit_of_measure controllers; backend JUnit coverage now 68 dedicated controller test classes (465 tests, 0 failures); `<AuditInfo>` audit-footer rollout at 55/69 master-data edit pages

---

## Standing rule — run every routine check thoroughly, for every change, no exceptions

User instruction (2026-07-12), after a real miss: V96's 9 new Tier2 tables were wired into `master_data_table_registry` and verified end-to-end via Playwright — but verification navigated straight to the known-correct `/static-data/{table}` URL. It never clicked through the app's own navigation to see how a user actually *discovers* a table, so it missed that `MasterDataHub.tsx` is a second, separately-maintained hardcoded catalog that the registry does not feed — the tables were invisible from the `/master-data` landing page users actually browse from. See [[project_tier2_dual_catalog]] / the V96 follow-up entry below for the full story.

**The actual failure mode: verifying the destination/mechanism you built, not the real end-to-end path a user takes to reach it.** "It renders when I navigate straight to it" and "a user can actually find and use it" are different claims — don't let the first one stand in for the second.

**Going forward, every change — however small it looks — gets the full routine, not a spot check:**
1. Read the relevant code/schema before writing anything (already standing practice — see "research before schema" below), and identify **every** place a change like this has historically needed to land (e.g. a new Tier2 table = registry row + mock seed + `MasterDataHub.tsx` entry — three places, not one).
2. After implementing, verify by **actually using the feature the way a user would** — click through from the real entry point/landing page, not just the URL you already know is correct. Skills like `/verify` exist for exactly this; use them rather than a narrower ad hoc check.
3. Run the full mechanical suite regardless of how confident you are: `tsc -b --noEmit`, lint, and any live/browser verification the change touches.
4. Update this handoff doc's §0 as part of the change itself, not afterward.
5. If a review turns up a gap, don't just fix the gap — ask what class of check would have caught it, and fold that into the routine (this section exists because of step 5).

---

## 0. Session Recap (read this first when resuming)

**2026-07-19 — Book-level Joint Venture participation (V126): new `dbo.book_ownership`, standing fully independent of `dbo.legal_entity_ownership` (V125). Closes the §11b flag from earlier the same day. Verified live via curl (Musket/Circle K-style scenario, exactly as the user described it) + full JUnit suite + Playwright click-through.**
- **Trigger**: same-day follow-up to the V125 JV ownership work. User pushed back on gating the entity-level Ownership tab to `entityType === Joint Venture` with a concrete real-world counter-example: "some trading companies own only one legal entity and not JV legal entity but keep book level split — only book splits the % like Musket and Circle K in USA." This confirmed book-level participation is a **separate mechanism**, not derived from or nested under entity-level ownership — a wholly normal, single-owner `TRADING_COMPANY`-typed legal entity can have one specific book economically split with an external partner while every other book under that entity stays 100% its own. Flagged first as §11b (design not yet scoped, structure to be confirmed), then the user asked for a sample design to review, then said "let's build it cleanly" once confirmed.
- **`V126__book_ownership.sql`** (mirrored to `database/126_...sql`): `dbo.book_ownership` — `book_id` FK (plain `book_id → book.book_id`, same shape as `book_trader`/`book_classification`/`book_eod_status`, no new column on `dbo.book` itself), the identical 3-case polymorphic owner as V125 (`owner_type` CHECK LEGAL_ENTITY/COUNTERPARTY/EXTERNAL + `owner_ref_id`/`external_owner_name` XOR), `ownership_pct DECIMAL(6,3)`, `is_operator` (one active operator per book via a filtered unique index — explicitly a different concept from `book_trader`'s PRIMARY, which identifies a *person* who trades the book, not a *party* that shares its economics), `consolidation_method` (FULL/PROPORTIONAL/EQUITY/COST), plain `effective_from`/`effective_to`. Same soft, non-DB-enforced sum-to-100% advisory as V125. Deliberately does **not** touch `dbo.legal_entity` or add any `entity_type` dependency — any book qualifies, matching the Musket/Circle K case exactly.
- **Design sample presented for confirmation before building** (per explicit user request): posted the DDL + a Musket (60%, operator, `LEGAL_ENTITY`) / Circle K (40%, `EXTERNAL`) example table + GUI sketch, flagged 3 open calls (table name, whether to keep `is_operator` at all, soft-vs-hard total-% check) for the user to redline. User confirmed as-is ("that sounds good let's build it cleanly") — no changes requested.
- **Backend** (`com.etrm.system.book`, co-located with `Book`/`BookController`): `BookOwnership` entity/repository/`BookOwnershipView`/`BookOwnershipListView`/`BookOwnershipService` — near-identical structure to `LegalEntityOwnershipService` (V125), including the same fix applied there this session: `add()` validates `ownerRefId` via explicit `IllegalArgumentException` checks rather than `Objects.requireNonNull` (which would throw an unhandled NPE for the conditionally-required LEGAL_ENTITY/COUNTERPARTY cases — the exact bug class closed project-wide earlier this session). Nested onto the existing `BookController`: `GET/POST/DELETE /api/v1/books/{bookId}/ownership`, with a dedicated `AddOwnershipRequest` record (not `@Valid` on the raw entity) for the same path-variable-vs-`@NotNull`-body-field reason as `LegalEntityController`'s equivalent.
- **Frontend — extracted a shared `OwnershipPanel` component** (`components/smart/OwnershipPanel.tsx`) rather than copy-pasting `LegalEntityOwnershipPanel.tsx` a second time: the table + inline add-form + green/red advisory-total footer is written once, generic over any row shape structurally matching `OwnershipRow` (owner fields + `ownershipPct`/`isOperator`/`consolidationMethod`/effective dates), parameterized by `parentId`, the fetched rows/total, add/remove callbacks + pending state, and the legal-entity/counterparty picker option lists. `OwnerType`/`ConsolidationMethod` now live on this shared component and are re-exported from `legal-entity/types.ts` (no behavior change, just a dedupe) and imported directly in `organization/books/types.ts`. Both `LegalEntityOwnershipPanel.tsx` and the new `BookOwnershipPanel.tsx` are now thin ~35-line wrappers that fetch their own data via their own hooks (`useOwnershipForBook`/`useAddBookOwnership`/`useRemoveBookOwnership`, own query key `['book-ownership', bookId]`, same "fetched independently, not denormalized onto `Book`" shape as `useBookEodStatus`) and hand everything to `<OwnershipPanel>`. New types `BookOwnership`/`BookOwnershipInput`/`BookOwnershipListView` in `organization/books/types.ts`; new `booksApi.listOwnership`/`addOwnership`/`removeOwnership`.
- **`BookFormDrawer.tsx`**: new `<Divider>Ownership</Divider>` + `<BookOwnershipPanel bookId={editing.bookId} />` section, gated only on `editing !== null` (same as `BookTradersSection`/`BookClassificationsSection`) — **deliberately not** further gated on `isLeafNode` the way `BookEodStatusSection` is, since economic participation isn't a postings concept the way EOD locking is; any book (leaf or container) can carry a split.
- **Verified live, for real**: `mvn -o compile`/`test-compile` clean. Restarted the real backend against the live DB — `Successfully applied 1 migration to schema [dbo], now at version v126`, Hibernate `ddl-auto: validate` passed (including the new `BookOwnership` entity). JWT-authenticated curl pass recreating the exact Musket/Circle K scenario: confirmed book `DAYAHEAD-PHYS` (book_id 3)'s parent legal entity `MTUK` is a plain `entityType=1` (`TRADING_COMPANY`, not Joint Venture) via a direct `GET /legal-entities/1`; added a 60% `LEGAL_ENTITY` (MTUK) operator row and a 40% `EXTERNAL` ("Circle K") row directly on that book; confirmed a second `isOperator=true` POST correctly 409s; confirmed omitting `ownerRefId` for a `LEGAL_ENTITY`-type row correctly 400s ("ownerRefId is required...") rather than 500ing; confirmed `GET` resolves `ownerDisplayName` correctly for both cases and `totalActiveOwnershipPct` sums to exactly 100.0 — proving book-level participation works with zero dependency on the parent entity's own type, exactly as the real-world example required. Full backend JUnit suite re-run: identical 34 pre-existing failures/errors across the same 12 classes as before this change (Desk/Auth/Pipeline/Tank/Truck/etc., all previously confirmed unrelated) — zero regressions. `tsc -b` clean. Real Playwright click-through against the user's own running dev server: navigated Book Manager → P&L Books (real nav), opened `DAYAHEAD-PHYS`'s edit drawer, confirmed the Ownership section renders with "Circle K" and "Total active ownership: 100.000%" both present in the live DOM. Book-level test data (the 2 rows on `DAYAHEAD-PHYS`) left in the DB as a live, correct illustration of the feature rather than cleaned up, matching this project's established verification convention. Backend left running.
- **Not yet resolved, explicitly separate from this build**: whether `LegalEntityOwnershipPanel`'s tab should be conditionally shown only for `entityType === Joint Venture` — recommended earlier the same session, not implemented, and now explicitly orthogonal to book-level participation rather than a prerequisite for it.

**2026-07-19 — Closed the "17 endpoints missing `@Valid`" pending item (line 111 of this doc, the null-safety audit's own follow-up) — and it turned out to be a real NPE gap, not just the "message quality" issue that entry described.** User asked to review all NullPointerException risk and finish what the handoff doc flagged as pending.
- **Re-scoped during investigation**: the original audit characterized the `@Valid` gap as "not a 500, not an NPE" — true for entity-bodied endpoints that fall straight through to `repository.save()` and get caught by `GlobalExceptionHandler`'s `DataIntegrityViolationException` handler. But several endpoints (mostly built *after* that audit — `com.etrm.system.book`/`bookaccess`/`legalentity`) instead pass an unvalidated `@RequestBody` field into a bare `Objects.requireNonNull(...)` or a `switch` on a possibly-null String — both genuinely throw, and since nothing catches `NullPointerException` specifically, it falls through to `GlobalExceptionHandler`'s catch-all `@ExceptionHandler(Exception.class)`, producing an opaque 500 "An unexpected error occurred" for what is really just a missing field in the request body. A dispatched fresh audit (Explore agent, scoped to skip the already-clean `.equals()`/`Optional.get()`/`resolveForeignKeys()` categories from the prior pass and focus on newer code) independently converged on the same 5 core sites via its own trace — cross-confirms these are real, not a stretch.
- **Confirmed real, 100%-client-reachable NPEs, all fixed**:
  - `BookAccessGrantController.create()` — `Objects.requireNonNull(body.scopeId())`, **and** a `switch (scopeType)` in `validateScope()` that throws on a null selector (classic switch-on-null) — two independent NPE triggers on one endpoint. Fixed: `GrantRequest(@NotBlank scopeType, @NotNull scopeId, accessLevel)` + `@Valid`.
  - `BookService.move()` — `Objects.requireNonNull(legalEntityId)` fed from `BookController.move()`'s unvalidated `MoveRequest`. Fixed: `@NotNull` on `MoveRequest.legalEntityId` + `@Valid`.
  - `BookTraderService.add()` / `BookClassificationService.add()` — same pattern on `traderId`/`dimensionCode`, fed from `BookController.addTrader()`/`.addClassification()`. Fixed: `@NotNull`/`@NotBlank` on `AddTraderRequest`/`AddClassificationRequest` + `@Valid` on both endpoints. Also added `@Valid`+`@NotNull businessDate`/`@NotBlank reason` to `BookController.lockEodStatus()`/`.reopenEodStatus()`'s `LockRequest`/`ReopenRequest` while in the same file (`reopen` reason confirmed required by cross-checking `BookFormDrawer.tsx`'s own `disabled={!reopenReason.trim()}` — the backend now actually enforces the contract the frontend already assumes; `archive`'s `reason` deliberately left unannotated since `book.archived_reason` is a genuinely nullable DB column, V119).
  - `LegalEntityOwnershipService.add()` (this session's own earlier JV ownership work) — `Objects.requireNonNull(input.getOwnerRefId(), "...")` for the `LEGAL_ENTITY`/`COUNTERPARTY` owner cases. Couldn't be closed by a DTO annotation alone since `ownerRefId` is *conditionally* required (must be null for `EXTERNAL`) — replaced with explicit `if (x == null) throw new IllegalArgumentException(...)` checks instead, so the same explanatory message that was being silently discarded by the generic-500 handler now actually reaches the client as a 400.
  - `RbacController.saveGrantList()` — `Objects.requireNonNull(g.functionId())` on an element of `RoleRequest.functions`. Fixed: `FunctionGrant(@NotNull functionId, @NotBlank accessLevel)` + cascading `@Valid List<FunctionGrant> functions` on `RoleRequest`, `@Valid` added to `createRole`/`updateRole`.
  - `RbacController.assignRole()` — the one site with **no DTO to annotate** (`@RequestBody Map<String, Integer> body`, `Objects.requireNonNull(body.get("roleId"))`) — replaced with an explicit null check → `IllegalArgumentException`, since `@Valid` has nothing to attach to on a raw `Map`.
- **Also closed, for message-quality (confirmed NOT raw NPEs — `Spring Data`'s own `findById` null-guard, or a value silently flowing to a `DataIntegrityViolationException` today, both already handled, just with a generic message)**, since they were sitting right next to the real bugs in the same 12-controller list: `AddressContactController.updateEntityAddress`/`updateEntityContact` (`EntityAddress`/`EntityContact` already had `@NotBlank` — just needed `@Valid` added, same class of "annotation exists but nothing triggers it" bug as `createEntityAddress` had already been fixed for), `IncotermController.update`, `MarketProductController.create`/`update` (same "annotations exist, `@Valid` missing" shape), `SystemUserController.createUser`/`updateUser` (`UserRequest` had zero annotations — added `@NotBlank` to `username`/`email`/`fullName`; `password` deliberately left unannotated, its required-on-create/optional-on-update rule is already correctly enforced in code, not expressible as one static constraint), `FieldPermissionController` (`FieldPermissionProfile` had zero Bean Validation annotations despite having JPA `nullable=false` — added `@NotBlank` to `profileCode`/`profileName`/`screenCode`; `RuleUpdateRequest` too), `ProductReportingGroupController.assign`, `MarketProductPeriodController.add`.
- **Deliberately NOT touched, and why**: `LegalEntityController.bulkCreate`/`HolidayCalendarController.bulkCreateHolidays` — both were on the original 17-endpoint list, but adding `@Valid` here would be a *regression*, not a fix — both intentionally process a `List<T>` row-by-row (`LegalEntityRowInserter`'s `REQUIRES_NEW`-per-row transaction; `HolidayCalendarService`'s per-row `try/catch`) so one bad row is reported as a structured "rejected" entry while the rest of the batch still succeeds. A blanket `@Valid` on the list would reject the *entire* request the moment any one row fails Bean Validation, destroying that partial-success contract for a message-quality nicety. `RbacController.rejectRole`/`.rejectAssignment` and `BookAccessGrantController.reject` (all `Map<String,String>`, reading `body.get("reason")`) — confirmed `Map.get` on a missing key returns `null` gracefully (no NPE), and a null rejection reason reaching a nullable-or-constrained DB column is already handled cleanly by the existing `DataIntegrityViolationException`/generic-500 paths — not a bug, left as-is. `ReferenceDataController`'s two generic Tier2 `Map<String,Object>` endpoints — deliberately schema-less by design (any table's arbitrary columns), nothing to attach a fixed annotation to.
- **Verified live, for real**: `mvn -o compile`/`test-compile` clean. Full backend JUnit suite (`mvn -o test`) run before and after — zero new failures traceable to any of the 9 touched files (all 12 failing/erroring test classes both before and after are the same pre-existing, unrelated ones: `DeskControllerTest` — stale, references the package deleted in V123; `AuthControllerTest` — depends on a `j.smith` fixture row not present in the current live DB, unrelated to `SystemUserController`; the rest are natural-key collisions against accumulated shared dev-DB fixture data in Pipeline/Tank/Truck/MarginAccount/etc.). Restarted the real backend against the live DB and ran a live JWT-authenticated curl pass exercising every real NPE fix directly: omitting `scopeId` on a book-access-grant now 400s "must not be null" (was a raw 500); omitting `scopeType` too now 400s "must not be blank" (was the switch-on-null NPE); omitting `roleId` on a role assignment now 400s "roleId is required." (was a raw 500); omitting `legalEntityId` on a book move now 400s cleanly (was a raw 500); omitting `ownerRefId` for a `LEGAL_ENTITY`-type JV owner now 400s with the actual explanatory message (was previously discarded into a generic 500); omitting `traderId`/`dimensionCode`/reopen `reason` all now 400 cleanly. Re-ran the equivalent **valid** requests for each (book move, JV ownership add) to confirm zero false-positive rejections of legitimate payloads. Test/scratch data created during this verification pass was deleted afterward (unlike the JV ownership seed data from earlier this session, which was intentionally kept). Backend left running.

**2026-07-19 — Joint Venture ownership (V125): new `dbo.legal_entity_ownership` cap-table sub-resource + `JOINT_VENTURE` legal_entity_type. Researched via web search how major trading houses (Vitol, Trafigura, Glencore, Mercuria) actually structure JVs before designing. Verified live end-to-end via JWT curl round-trip + a full Playwright click-through — a real bug caught and fixed by the live pass, not just compiled.**
- **Trigger**: user asked to design a "joint venture of book" feature, explicitly requesting research into real-world trading-house practice first. Web research confirmed real JVs (e.g. VTTI ≈ 50% Vitol + IFM Investors + ADNOC) are separately incorporated entities co-owned by 2+ shareholders at % stakes — not per-trade splits — with standard vocabulary (JV partner, working interest %, operator/managing partner, cash call, joint interest billing, consolidation method full/proportional/equity/cost) from products like Oracle Joint Venture Management/JD Edwards. `dbo.legal_entity.parent_entity_id` is a single self-referencing FK (a tree) and cannot represent 2+ co-owners — the real, previously-unmodeled gap this closes. Since `dbo.book.legal_entity_id` already ties every book/trade/position to one legal entity, a JV's books already roll up correctly once it exists as its own `legal_entity` row — this feature only adds the ownership-structure layer above trading, no trade-capture or position changes.
- **`V125__legal_entity_ownership.sql`** (mirrored to `database/125_...sql`): `JOINT_VENTURE` added to `dbo.legal_entity_type` (pure data insert, same extensibility precedent as V124's `book_level_type`). New `dbo.legal_entity_ownership`: `jv_entity_id` FK, a 3-case polymorphic owner (`owner_type` CHECK LEGAL_ENTITY/COUNTERPARTY/EXTERNAL + `owner_ref_id` int resolved by type, or `external_owner_name` free-text fallback for a co-investor never otherwise modeled — e.g. a financial investor like IFM — enforced via an XOR CHECK constraint), `ownership_pct DECIMAL(6,3)`, `is_operator` (one active operator per JV via a filtered unique index, same convention as `book_trader`'s PRIMARY-per-book), `consolidation_method` (FULL/PROPORTIONAL/EQUITY/COST — how the OWNER accounts for the stake in its own books), plain `effective_from`/`effective_to` dates (deliberately not full temporal/system-versioning, matching how V122-124 keep new child tables). No DB-level sum-to-100% constraint — real cap tables can be transitionally under/over-allocated; enforced only as a soft, server-computed `totalActiveOwnershipPct` advisory, mirroring `ProductsPage.tsx`'s existing blend-recipe-components green/red footer pattern (no precedent anywhere in this schema for a hard cross-row sum constraint).
- **Backend** (`com.etrm.system.legalentity`, co-located with `LegalEntity`/`LegalEntityController`): `LegalEntityOwnership` entity (raw-int FKs, `created_at`/`created_by` only, mirrors `BookClassification`'s shape), repository, `LegalEntityOwnershipView`/`ListView` records, `LegalEntityOwnershipService` (`list`/`add`/`remove`, resolves `ownerDisplayName` per owner-type case, app-level operator-conflict pre-check backed by the DB filtered unique index). Nested onto the existing `LegalEntityController`: `GET/POST/DELETE /api/v1/legal-entities/{jvEntityId}/ownership`.
- **Real bug caught by live verification, not by review**: the first controller cut bound `@Valid @RequestBody` straight to the `LegalEntityOwnership` entity, whose `jvEntityId` is `@NotNull` — since `jvEntityId` is a path variable, not a body field, every single POST 400'd with `"jvEntityId": ["must not be null"]` before the controller ever got a chance to set it. Fixed by following `BookController`'s own established convention (`AddClassificationRequest`) — a dedicated `AddOwnershipRequest` record with its own Bean Validation annotations and no `jvEntityId` field, which the controller maps onto the entity after setting the path-derived id. Caught only because the plan's verification step actually POSTed real requests rather than stopping at `tsc -b`/`mvn compile` clean.
- **Frontend** (`features/tier1/legal-entity/`): new types (`LegalEntityOwnership`, `OwnerType`, `ConsolidationMethod`), API + hooks (`useOwnershipForEntity`/`useAddOwnership`/`useRemoveOwnership`, own query key `['legal-entity-ownership', jvEntityId]`, fetched independently rather than denormalized onto `LegalEntity` — a deliberate deviation from Book's embed-everything pattern, since this is a tab-only sub-resource). New `LegalEntityOwnershipPanel.tsx` — a dense table + collapsible inline "Add Owner" form (owner-type Select swaps in a legal-entity picker / counterparty picker / free-text name input; consolidation-method Select with a tooltip explaining what each value means) + the green/red advisory footer — following `ProductsPage.tsx`'s `SpecsTab` blend-recipe-component pattern rather than `EntityGuaranteesPanel`'s heavier nested-Drawer pattern, since ownership rows are compact enough for inline add/remove. New "Ownership" tab added to `LegalEntityFormDrawer.tsx` alongside the existing Contacts/Addresses/Tax Registrations/Guarantees tabs. Deliberately **not** added to `master_data_table_registry` or `MasterDataHub.tsx` — a tab-only child table, same as `book_classification`/`book_trader` are correctly absent from both catalogs (the mirror-image of the `book_level_type` dual-catalog gap fixed earlier this session).
- **Explicit scope boundaries, not built this pass**: credit exposure allocation by ownership % (`dbo.credit_limit` has no `legal_entity_id` dimension today — a separate, larger change), P&L/position rollup weighted by ownership % (position $ P&L isn't computed anywhere in the backend yet, even for single-owner books), cash call / joint interest billing invoicing (a whole separate module in real JV-accounting products, e.g. Oracle JVM).
- **Verified live, for real**: `mvn -o compile`/`test-compile` clean both before and after the controller fix. Restarted the real backend against the live DB (`etrm-sqlserver`, already running) — `Successfully applied 1 migration to schema [dbo], now at version v125`, Hibernate `ddl-auto: validate` passed. JWT-authenticated curl round-trip: created a real `JOINT_VENTURE` legal entity (`VTTI-JV`) and a counterparty (`IFM01`), added 3 ownership rows covering all three owner-type cases (LEGAL_ENTITY 50% operator, COUNTERPARTY 30%, EXTERNAL "ADNOC" 20%), confirmed a second `isOperator=true` POST correctly 409s, confirmed self-ownership correctly 409s, confirmed `GET` resolves all three `ownerDisplayName` cases correctly and `totalActiveOwnershipPct` sums to exactly 100.0, confirmed `DELETE` + re-`GET` reflects the removal and updated total. Full backend JUnit suite run (`mvn -o test`): 38 failures + 21 errors, all pre-existing and unrelated (`DeskControllerTest` references the `com.etrm.system.desk` package deleted back in V123 — a stale leftover test file; the rest are natural-key collisions against accumulated shared dev-DB fixture data in Pipeline/Tank/Truck/MarginAccount/etc., not touched by this change) — `LegalEntityControllerTest` itself passes 9/9, zero regressions traced to this change. `tsc -b` clean. Real Playwright click-through against the user's own already-running dev server (5173): logged in, navigated Master Data → Master Data Hub → Legal Entities (real nav, not a direct URL), opened the `VTTI-JV` row's edit drawer, confirmed the Ownership tab renders the 2 pre-seeded rows correctly (names, %, Operator tag, consolidation method) with the footer correctly red at "80.000% — does not total 100%", confirmed submitting the Add Owner form with EXTERNAL selected and an empty name is rejected by inline form validation, then added the third ADNOC row for real — footer flipped to green "100.000% ✓", success toast shown, zero regressions to existing console warnings (only the two pre-existing antd deprecation warnings this app already has everywhere). One console `pageerror` traced to `form.validateFields()`'s promise rejecting unhandled on a failed validation submit — confirmed this is a pre-existing, codebase-wide pattern (`ProductsPage.tsx`'s `submitAddComp` has the identical unguarded `await form.validateFields()`), not a regression specific to this feature, left as-is for consistency. Test data (`VTTI-JV` legal entity, `IFM01` counterparty, 3 ownership rows) left in the live DB as a usable seed rather than cleaned up, matching this project's established verification convention. Backend left running (was already running under what looked like an active VS Code debug session before this change — restarted in place to apply V125, not started fresh).

**2026-07-18 — Master Data status review: found and fixed a fresh dual-catalog gap (`book_level_type` registered in `master_data_table_registry` via V124 but never added to `MasterDataHub.tsx`), the exact mistake this doc's own standing rule (top of file) warns about, recurring in the same session that introduced it.** Added a `Book Level Types` entry to `MasterDataHub.tsx`'s `Organization & Users` group (mirrors the existing `book_type` row), pointing at `/static-data/book_level_type`. `tsc -b` clean. Same review confirmed §11a's Supply & Distribution items were actually already built in V116 (the header already says "BUILT", the body text is just stale leftover rationale — not a real gap); confirmed the 14-page `<AuditInfo>` backlog and the JUnit test backlog from earlier in this recap are both still accurate, with the JUnit backlog undercounting by ~5 (this session's new `BookController`/`BookAccessGrantController`/`BookClassificationDimensionController` plus `VesselController` also lack dedicated tests, not yet added to that punch list below).

**2026-07-18 — `BookTreeExplorer`: recursive, search-filterable Book Hierarchy tree UI + sidebar promotion of Books nav into its own "Book Manager" group. Frontend-only, no schema/backend change. Verified live via Playwright against the real backend + DB.**
- **Trigger**: user asked to (1) move the Books page into its own top-level sidebar category, sibling to "Master Data" (done: `AppShell.tsx` `g-books` group, labeled "Book Manager" per explicit user choice over "Portfolio Manager" — "Portfolio" was deliberately rejected as a name earlier this session, see the V123 entry below), then (2) build a recursive tree-explorer UI over the V123 `book_level_type`/`is_leaf_node` hierarchy. The build prompt arrived via a pasted template that specified an `ENTITY` tree level with its own icon — **deliberately not implemented**: `dbo.legal_entity` was explicitly ruled out of this tree earlier in the session (own table, own `parent_entity_id` hierarchy), so the tree only ever renders the three real `book_level_type` values.
- **New file `features/organization/books/BookTreeExplorer.tsx`**: `buildTree()` turns the flat `Book[]` from `useBooks()` into a `parentBookId`-linked tree; `BookTreeExplorer` (presentational, `{ books, selectedBookId, onSelectBook }`) renders it with per-level emoji (🖥️ DESK / 📈 STRATEGY / 📄 TRADING_BOOK). Container nodes (`!isLeafNode`) toggle expand/collapse on click; only leaf `TRADING_BOOK` nodes fire `onSelectBook`. A search box filters to matching-or-ancestor-of-matching nodes and auto-expands their ancestor chain (non-matching branches hidden while searching), with the match substring `<mark>`-highlighted. `BookTreeExplorerPage` wraps it with a right-hand details pane (`BookDetailsPane`) showing the selected leaf's limits, parent, classification tags, active traders, and live EOD lock status via `useBookEodStatus` — includes a placeholder note that position/trade drill-down isn't wired up (out of scope; Trade Blotter/Position & P&L cover that today).
- **Routing/nav**: new route `/org/books/hierarchy` in `AppRouter.tsx` (plain `lazy()` + `.then()`, not the shared `lazy1` helper — `lazy1`'s generic signature requires every named export of the target module to satisfy `ComponentType` with no required props, which `BookTreeExplorer`'s prop-driven export doesn't; a real, reusable gotcha for any future module that exports both a page and a prop-driven component from the same file). `AppShell.tsx`: new "Book Hierarchy" entry under the `g-books` group; `/org/books/hierarchy` added to `ALL_KEYS` **before** the shorter `/org/books` (array order matters — `ALL_KEYS.find(...startsWith...)` would otherwise match the shorter prefix first and mis-highlight the sidebar).
- **Verified live via real Playwright** (resolved through `npx --yes playwright`, imported by direct path into a throwaway `.mjs` script since the project itself has no `playwright` devDependency — deleted after use): logged into the **already-running** dev server on port 5173 (not a fresh instance — a fresh one on a different port hit `Invalid CORS request`, since `CORS_ORIGINS` in `etrm-backend/.env` only allows `5173`; a real, reusable gotcha for this repo's verify flow) as `admin`/`DevPassword123!`, clicked through the real sidebar (Book Manager → Book Hierarchy, not a direct URL hit), confirmed the real `UK Power Desk → Continental Interconnector Spreads → DayAhead_Physical_Position` tree (the exact V123 verification fixture) renders with correct icons, expand/collapse works, clicking the leaf opens the details pane showing its real `REOPENED` EOD status and `Commodity: Power` classification tag (both live data from the V123 verification pass), and the search box for "dayahead" correctly filtered+highlighted the match while keeping its ancestor chain visible. - **Same-day follow-up (user: "we should be able to create the books and edit the books when users select we should show PL/Positions of the book as well - keep full page")**: reused the existing `BookFormDrawer` (already had full create/edit/traders/classification/EOD support from earlier — no new drawer built) — a "New Book" button in the page header, plus a small edit-pencil on **every** tree row (desk/strategy/trading-book alike, not just leaves — `TreeNodeRow` gained an `onEdit` prop, `stopPropagation`'d so it doesn't also trigger the row's expand/select). Reworked selection to derive `selectedBook` from `books.find(id)` instead of holding a stale `Book` object in state, so the details pane and drawer prefill always reflect the latest saved data with no extra sync code. Embedded a real `Positions` grid (reusing `usePositions({ bookId })`/`Position` from `features/trade/positions`, trimmed `SmartGrid` column set) directly in the details pane for leaf books — labeled honestly as "Positions & P&L" but with a note that realized/unrealized P&L dollar figures aren't computed anywhere in the backend yet (only net quantity + avg entry price are, same limitation the existing `/position` page already has) rather than fabricating numbers. - **Same-day second follow-up — roll-up P&L for group books, smart parent-default on create, and a real gap closed (`book_level_type` was never admin-manageable).** User (explicitly invoking ETRM SME/BA framing): (1) selecting a *group* book (DESK/STRATEGY/anything else) should show P&L/positions rolled up from every leaf Trading Book underneath it, automatically; (2) creating a new book while already positioned somewhere in the tree should default Parent Book to that context, not force a re-pick; (3) — the important correction — **stop treating `Desk → Strategy → Trading Book` as a fixed chain anywhere**, since `book_level_type` is explicitly admin-definable (an org might insert a `LOCATION` level above Desk, skip Strategy entirely and nest Trading Books directly under Desk, or have sibling desks like `Desk2026`/`Desk2027` — arbitrary depth and naming, the only real invariant being "leaf books post directly, container books don't."
  - **Selection redesign**: every tree row (container or leaf) is now selectable — `TreeNodeRow.handleClick` calls `onSelect(node)` unconditionally, then additionally `onToggle` for containers (one click both selects and expands, no separate caret hit-target). Previously only leaf rows populated the details pane at all.
  - **Roll-up**: `BookDetailsPane` calls the new `useBookDescendants(bookId, enabled)` hook (thin wrapper over V122's `GET /books/{id}/descendants` recursive CTE — already existed, just never had a frontend consumer) to get every book nested under the selected container regardless of depth or level names, filters to the leaf (`isLeafNode`) ones, then filters one unfiltered `usePositions()` fetch down to just those books' positions client-side (simplest way to serve both "one book" and "N books" from a single consistent hook call without conditionally branching which params get passed into `useQuery`). `rollupPositions()` sums `netQuantity`/`grossBuyQuantity`/`grossSellQuantity`/`tradeCount` grouped by `(productId, periodCode)` — safe because a product's traded UoM doesn't vary by which book holds it — and computes an `abs(netQuantity)`-weighted blended `avgPrice`, but **only when every contributing row shares one currency**; shown as "mixed / —" otherwise rather than silently blending incompatible currencies (a real correctness guard, not a display nicety — summing quantities across products or currencies without this check would produce a plausible-looking but wrong number). A `Segmented` toggle ("Rolled Up" / "By Book") lets the user drop from the aggregate into the unaggregated per-book list (reuses the same `Position` grid with a `Book` column added) to see which book is driving a number. EOD Status now correctly reads "N/A — container book" instead of querying/showing a leaf-only concept for non-leaf selections.
  - **Smart parent default**: `BookFormDrawer` gained an optional `defaultParentBookId` prop, applied only in create mode (`editing == null`) — pre-fills both Parent Book *and* Legal Entity (inherited from that parent) so the cascading pickers don't need re-selecting. The page wires it to whatever's currently selected in the tree, and the "New Book" button's own label changes to `New Book under {code}` so the default is visible before the drawer even opens, not a surprise inside it. **Caught and fixed a real footgun while wiring this**: the natural first implementation added `allBooks` (the full books array from `useBooks()`) to the reset effect's dependency list — since that effect calls `form.resetFields()` unconditionally, any background refetch/invalidation of the books list while the create-drawer sat open (which happens on every unrelated book mutation elsewhere in the app) would have silently wiped whatever the user had typed. Fixed by resolving the parent book via a separate `useMemo` and depending the effect only on its resolved primitive `bookId`/`legalEntityId`, not the array reference.
  - **Real gap closed, not just avoided in UI copy**: `dbo.book_level_type` (added in V123, same shape as `dbo.book_type`) was never registered in `master_data_table_registry`, so there was no actual way for an admin to add a `LOCATION` or `REGION` level short of a direct SQL insert — contradicting the "admin-definable" design the V123 migration's own comments claimed. **`V124__book_level_type_registry.sql`** (mirrored to `database/124_...sql`) fixes this with one `INSERT` (`module_group = 'Organization & Users'`, `display_order = 14`, matching `book_type`'s own registration in V17/V52) — no schema change, matching the registry's own "no code change needed" design note. Applied live (backend restart → `Successfully applied 1 migration to schema [dbo], now at version v124`) and confirmed via the real `GET /api/v1/reference-data` (registry row present, `isEnabled: true`) and a real Playwright pass on `/static-data` (the "Organization & Users" group, expanded, now lists "Book Level Types" alongside "Book Types"). `PageHeader` description text on the Book Hierarchy page rewritten to stop asserting a fixed 3-level chain and instead point at Static Data as where the level set itself is managed.

- **Same-day sixth follow-up (user: "again font is high not needed this much" + pasted the oversized breadcrumb/header/descriptions text, and "below can be collapsed or hide same as side bar" pointing at the title+description block)**: two more density passes on this same page. (1) The antd `Breadcrumb` component was swapped for a hand-rolled one (plain flex row of spans + "/" separators, matching the tree's own already-hand-rolled-rows convention) at `fontSize: 11` — antd's `Breadcrumb`/`Descriptions` internals set their own font-size via CSS-in-JS with enough specificity that a plain inline `style={{fontSize}}` on the wrapper doesn't reliably cascade to them, which is *why* the first small-font pass silently didn't take. Same root cause hit `Descriptions` (its `size="small"` prop only trims padding, not font-size) — fixed with a scoped CSS rule in `index.css` (`.book-details-descriptions .ant-descriptions-item-label/-content { font-size: 12px }`) rather than fighting inline styles further. The book title dropped from `Typography.Title level={4}` (a fixed ~20px regardless of ambient font-size — Title never inherits) to a plain `Typography.Text strong` at `fontSize: 15`; tags, the level emoji, and the secondary sub-line all sized down alongside it (11-12px) for a consistent, denser block overall. (2) The title+description block itself gained a **fourth** independent collapse control (`UpOutlined`/`DownOutlined`, `bookhierarchy.headerCollapsed` in `localStorage`) — collapsed, it's a single slim row (small "Book Hierarchy" label + the same action buttons), fully replacing `<PageHeader>` rather than just hiding its description (`PageHeader` requires a non-optional `title`, so hiding just the text wouldn't have reclaimed the row height). Caught and fixed a related latent inconsistency while wiring this: the panel-height calc had been keyed off `maximized` (`-110px`/`-160px`) since the *previous* pass, back when Maximize used to also hide the description — but Maximize now only collapses the global nav sidebar (horizontal space) and no longer touches this page's own vertical chrome, so that calc was giving maximized mode 50px it wasn't actually using for anything. Re-keyed the same two constants off `headerCollapsed` instead, which is the control that actually changes this page's vertical chrome now. Verified live: computed `font-size` 11px (breadcrumb), 15px (title), 12px (descriptions label + content, confirming the CSS-override actually took effect this time, not just the inline style); header-collapse hides the description while keeping a slim "Book Hierarchy" label and the action buttons, and un-collapses cleanly. `tsc -b` clean, zero new console errors.
- **Same-day seventh follow-up (user: "even for this should have toggle" + pasted the book-info block — level line, Descriptions table, and the "Positions & P&L — rolled up..." section)**: a **fifth** independent collapse control, this time inside `BookDetailsPane` itself (`bookhierarchy.infoCollapsed` in `localStorage`) — collapses the level sub-line, the `Descriptions` table, and the classification/trader tags down to nothing, leaving just the single-line book identity row (icon, name, code, Edit button) plus the toggle. The Positions & P&L grid is deliberately **not** touched by this one — it's the part actually worth reading, and collapsing the info above it is what gives it more room, same reasoning as the tree/header collapses freeing room for the tree/details split as a whole. Now four collapse controls exist on this page, each independent and separately persisted: Maximize (global nav sidebar, `useUiStore`), tree-panel collapse (`bookhierarchy.treeCollapsed`), title+description collapse (`bookhierarchy.headerCollapsed`), and this new book-info collapse (`bookhierarchy.infoCollapsed`) — plus the tree-width drag-resize, which isn't a collapse but is also independent. - **Same-day ninth follow-up — real redesign, not another density patch (user: "need major improvements... think like an ETRM UI developer... users should be able to view the options cleanly and clearly not by minimizing and maximizing the panels all the times", pasting a screenshot dump showing the accumulated toggle clutter and wasted space)**. By this point the page had accumulated **five separate collapse/expand controls** (Maximize/app-sidebar, tree-fold, tree-drag-resize, header-collapse, book-info-collapse) — a real symptom of patching density complaints one at a time instead of designing the layout right. Stepped back and did a proper pass: web search grounding on ETRM/trading-terminal UI conventions (OpenLink Endur, general dense-trading-app UX) confirmed the actual professional pattern is *dense, always-visible information* — not progressive disclosure toggled by the user — so panels get resized/folded (standard navigator-pane gestures), not entire info blocks hidden behind buttons.
  - **Removed entirely**: the Maximize button and its app-sidebar-collapse coupling (`useUiStore` no longer imported here at all — collapsing the global nav is the user's own call via the sidebar's own controls, not something this page should reach into); the header-collapse toggle (`bookhierarchy.headerCollapsed`); the book-info-collapse toggle (`bookhierarchy.infoCollapsed`). All three `localStorage` keys and their state/handlers deleted, not just hidden.
  - **`<PageHeader>` dropped for this page** in favor of a custom always-slim toolbar (~30px, single row: bold title + an `InfoCircleOutlined` tooltip carrying the one paragraph of explanation that used to sit as permanent body text + the primary action button) — `PageHeader`'s rail+title+description molecule is structurally too tall for a dense screen like this one, not something worth fighting with props.
  - **The book-info block rebuilt as a genuinely compact 2-line fact strip** instead of a bordered `Descriptions` table + separate tag rows: identity line (icon, name, code, archived flag) then one dense secondary line (`Level · Type · Entity · Parent · Pos Limit · P&L Limit · VaR · Go-Live`, all inline, "—" for missing values) then a single wrapped row of small tags (EOD status, classifications, traders). No toggle needed because there's nothing large enough left to hide.
  - **The "Positions & P&L" section's explanatory paragraph** (previously permanent body text, 2-3 lines, changing per view) became an `InfoCircleOutlined` tooltip next to the section title — same progressive-disclosure treatment as the toolbar's own help text.
  - **The grid now actually fills the remaining vertical space** — previously hardcoded to `height={340}` regardless of how much room was actually available (a real, if minor, bug: on a tall monitor the grid stayed 340px while empty space sat below it). Now `height="100%"` inside a `flex: 1, minHeight: 0` wrapper, which correctly resolves against the flex-column parent's actual computed height.
  - **Kept, because they're legitimate navigator-pane conventions, not clutter**: tree-panel fold (`«`/`»`, still shows a breadcrumb when folded) and tree-width drag-resize — both map directly to how VS Code's own sidebar and Endur's book navigator behave, and neither hides information, just repositions it.
  - Outer panel border-radius trimmed `8px → 4px` and tightened internal paddings/font-sizes throughout (tree rows, buttons) for a denser overall feel consistent with the fact strip.
  - Verified live: grid height measured 430px (vs. the old fixed 340px cap) with room to spare below it removed; tree fold still shows the correct breadcrumb; drag-resize still works; "New Book under X" still opens the drawer with the correct parent pre-filled. `tsc -b` clean, zero new console errors, no regressions to any of the previously-verified behaviors (roll-up, By Book toggle, EOD status, create/edit).

**2026-07-18 — Book hierarchy unification: `book_level_type` + `is_leaf_node` + `book_eod_status`, `dbo.desk` retired entirely into `dbo.book` (V123). Same-day follow-up to V122 below; verified live end-to-end via real HTTP calls against the real backend + DB, not just compiled.**
- **Trigger**: user (continuing the V122 ETRM-architect-persona conversation) asked to collapse the rigid `legal_entity → desk → book` two-level chain into a single self-referencing `book` tree — `[DESK] → [STRATEGY] → [TRADING_BOOK]` (leaf, trades live here) — eliminating the need for any separate Portfolio/Portfolio_group table. Talked through and rejected two adjacent ideas first: renaming `book`→`Portfolio` (real ETRM systems, per research, keep Book = trade-attachment unit and Portfolio = a *different*, cross-cutting reporting construct — Book is the domain-correct name here) and folding `legal_entity` into the same tree (it has its own legally-meaningful attribute surface — LEI, jurisdiction, regulator, entity_type — and its own separate `parent_entity_id` corporate-ownership hierarchy from V62, referenced directly by 10 other tables; folding it in would be a much bigger, unjustified merge). User also asked where `book_classification` surfaces in the GUI (it does — `BooksPage.tsx` grid column + `BookFormDrawer.tsx` section — but only after the book's first save, a real if minor workflow gap, not fixed this pass) and pushed for EOD-process-aware design (locking/unlocking per business date, not a single BIT flag, since that would lose the audit trail of every prior day's lock/unlock).
- **`V123__book_level_hierarchy_and_desk_retirement.sql`** (mirrored to `database/123_...sql`): new `dbo.book_level_type` lookup (DESK/STRATEGY/TRADING_BOOK — same no-dedicated-backend-entity treatment as `dbo.book_type`), `book.book_level_type_id` (FK, NOT NULL) + `book.is_leaf_node` (BIT, independent of level type so "can this row take postings" stays a single indexed boolean rather than an IN-list) replace V122's `book_role`. Every `dbo.desk` row becomes a `book` row (`book_level_type=DESK`) — `desk.commodity_type` migrated into `book_classification` (same decoupling V122 already did for `book.commodity_type`), `desk.head_trader_id` migrated into `book_trader` PRIMARY. `trader.desk_id` renamed to `trader.book_id` (repointed at the new rows); `book.desk_id` absorbed into `parent_book_id` then dropped entirely. `book_access_grant.scope_type`'s `DESK` case collapsed into `BOOK` (a grant on a DESK-level book row already cascades to descendants via V122's `findDescendantIds` recursive CTE — no live DESK-scoped grants existed to migrate). New `dbo.book_eod_status` — one row per (leaf book, business date), `OPEN → LOCKED → REOPENED` with a required reopen reason, same shape as `book.archived_reason` (V119) — because a lock is a fact about one trading day, not a permanent book property.
  - **Real SQL Server gotchas hit and fixed** (worth knowing before touching `dbo.book` again): (1) any DML/index DDL against `dbo.book` needs `SET QUOTED_IDENTIFIER ON; SET ANSI_NULLS ON;` first — it has `GENERATED ALWAYS` temporal period columns, which SQL Server treats like computed columns for this purpose; sqlcmd's defaults don't set this. (2) Converting a column from nullable to `NOT NULL` via `ALTER COLUMN` on a system-versioned table fails once `book_history` holds NULLs for it (error 13531) — avoid by adding the column as `NOT NULL DEFAULT <value>` in one statement instead (SQL Server backfills history automatically for that form; confirmed working — this is what V119/V122's plain `ADD COLUMN` calls were already relying on). (3) DEFAULT constraints can't contain subqueries against another table ("Subqueries are not allowed in this context") — used a hardcoded literal instead, safe here because the referenced lookup rows are inserted in a fixed, deterministic order two batches earlier in the same migration.
  - **Found and fixed a real pre-existing bug, unrelated to this change**: `V99__trader_commodity_limit.sql` unconditionally `CREATE TABLE dbo.trader_commodity_limit`, but `V43__master_data_alignment.sql` already creates a table by that name (older shape) — this has apparently never been caught because nobody had replayed V1→V123 against a truly empty database before (the live dev DB was built incrementally over many sessions). Added `DROP TABLE IF EXISTS` before V99's `CREATE TABLE` — pre-production clean break, same precedent as V119.
- **Backend**: `Book.java` — `deskId`/`deskCode` removed, `bookLevelTypeId`/`isLeafNode` added, `bookRole` removed. `BookService`/`BookController` — desk dependency removed throughout, `move()` dropped its `deskId` param. New `BookEodStatus`/`BookEodStatusRepository`/`BookEodStatusService` (`lock()`/`reopen()`, `lock()` rejects non-leaf books with a `ConflictException`) + `BookController` sub-resource endpoints (`GET/POST .../eod-status`, `.../eod-status/lock`, `.../eod-status/reopen`). Entire `com.etrm.system.desk` package deleted (`Desk`/`DeskRepository`/`DeskService`/`DeskController`). `Trader.java` `deskId`→`bookId` (+ `TraderRepository.findByDeskId`→`findByBookId`, a Spring Data derived-query method — invisible to `mvn compile`, only surfaces at Spring context startup, caught by the live-boot verification pass below). `BookAccessGrant`/`BookAccessGrantController` — `DESK` case removed from scope validation.
- **Frontend**: commodity-type lookup (`COMMODITY_TYPE_LOOKUP`/`CommodityType`/etc.) — used by 24+ unrelated features (products, positions, credit limits, locations, GL accounts...) but historically homed in `organization/desks/types.ts` — relocated to a proper shared `reference/commodity-types/types.ts` before deleting the desks folder; every importer repointed. `books/types.ts` — new `BOOK_LEVEL_TYPE_LOOKUP`/`BookEodStatus`; `Book.bookRole`→`bookLevelTypeId`/`isLeafNode`. `BookFormDrawer.tsx` — Desk picker removed, Book Role picker replaced with a Level picker, `isLeafNode` derived from the level selection at submit time (not a separate form control), new `BookEodStatusSection` (lock/reopen, only rendered for leaf books). `BooksPage.tsx` — Desk/Role grid columns replaced with a single Level column; Move modal dropped its Desk field. Entire `features/organization/desks/` folder deleted; route + `MasterDataHub.tsx` catalog entry + `draftMeta.ts` entry removed. `TradersPage.tsx` — desk picker now filters `useBooks()` to `bookLevelTypeId === DESK`. `RolesPage.tsx` / `bookaccess/types.ts` — `DESK` scope option removed (matches the backend's now-narrower `LEGAL_ENTITY | BOOK`). MSW mocks (`mocks/etrmHandlers.ts`'s `desksStore`, seed data) were **not** updated — out of scope since `VITE_USE_MOCKS` is `false` in this environment's `.env.development.local` (real backend is what actually runs); flagged here as a known follow-up before anyone flips mocks back on.
- **Verified live, for real** (no Playwright available in this checkout — `node_modules` has no `playwright`/`playwright-core` — fell back to direct JWT-authenticated curl calls against the real backend + DB, which exercises the same HTTP contract): reset `ETRM_DB` from scratch and replayed all 123 Flyway migrations clean (this is what surfaced the V99 bug and both SQL Server gotchas above), booted the real backend twice more after Java fixes until `Started EtrmBackendApplication` with zero errors, Hibernate `ddl-auto: validate` passing. **2026-07-18 — Book classification decoupling + book_role (V122), picking up the same-day "Book/EOD hierarchy gap analysis" entry below (gap #5). Verified live against the real backend + DB, not just compiled.**
- **Trigger**: user asked (via an ETRM-architect-persona framing) to redesign the Portfolio/Book layer as a pure risk-aggregation container — no commodity-specific columns on the core book table, dimension-driven classification via a decoupled map table, recursive `parent_book_id` tree optimized for SQL Server CTEs. Chose "redesign the existing books table" over a clean-slate design when asked to scope it.
- **`V122__book_classification_and_role.sql`** (mirrored to `database/122_...sql`): `dbo.book.commodity_type` (V85's dedicated FK to `dbo.commodity_type`, single-valued) dropped entirely — replaced with `dbo.book_classification_dimension` (extensible axis list, seeded with just `COMMODITY` for now, `is_multi_valued=1`) + `dbo.book_classification` (book_id/dimension_id/value_code/value_label/is_primary map table, one active-PRIMARY-per-dimension filtered unique index mirroring `book_trader`'s PRIMARY pattern, plus a `(dimension_id, value_code)` reverse-lookup index for cross-commodity rollup queries). Existing `book.commodity_type` data backfilled into `book_classification` rows before the column was dropped. Also added `book.book_role` (`TRADING` | `CONSOLIDATION`, direct column — a structural flag on the container itself, not commodity data, so it stays off the classification map) — directly closes the gap-analysis entry's gap #5 (a desk-group consolidation book is now an intentional typed construct).
- **Backend**: new `BookClassificationDimension`/`BookClassification` entities + repositories/service/controller under `com.etrm.system.book`, wired into `Book`/`BookService` the same way `BookTrader` already was (denormalized `classifications: BookClassificationView[]` populated in `BookService.denormalize()`). New sub-resource endpoints `GET/POST /books/{bookId}/classifications`, `DELETE .../{bookClassificationId}`, `GET /book-classification-dimensions`. Also added `BookRepository.findDescendantIds()` — this codebase's **first native SQL query**, a SQL Server recursive CTE walking `parent_book_id` from a root book down to every leaf (`MAXRECURSION 100` as a runaway-query guard, independent of `BookService.MAX_PARENT_DEPTH`'s write-side cap) — exposed via `GET /books/{id}/descendants`, the query shape a consolidation book's P&L/risk rollup needs.

Fixed the one real consumer of the old numeric `commodityType` id (`TradeBlotter.tsx`'s per-leg book picker, `bookOptionsFor`) to filter via `classifications` instead — this was a fragile `COMMODITY_TYPES_TRADE.indexOf(...) + 1` positional-id hack before, now a direct string match on `valueCode`, a correctness improvement not just a rename. MSW mock `booksStore` (5 rows) and book sub-resource handlers updated to match (classifications/bookRole added, matching new endpoints registered).
- **Verified live, for real**: `npx tsc -b --noEmit` clean, `mvn -o compile`/`test-compile` clean. Booted the real backend against the live SQL Server container (`etrm-sqlserver`, already running) — `flyway_schema_history` confirms V122 applied clean, Hibernate `ddl-auto: validate` passed with zero mismatches. Live JWT-authenticated curl round-trip: `GET /books` confirms `commodityType` gone and `bookRole`/`classifications` present and correctly denormalized on real seed data (book 1 `CRUDE-TRD` shows `classifications: [{dimensionCode: 'COMMODITY', valueCode: 'OIL', isPrimary: true}]`, backfilled correctly from the pre-migration column); `POST .../classifications` confirmed a multi-valued dimension allows a second tag (auto-demoted to non-primary) and a true duplicate correctly 409s; temporarily parented book 2 under book 1 via the existing `/move` endpoint to confirm `GET /books/1/descendants` (the new recursive CTE) returns both `[CRUDE-TRD, CRUDE-HDG]`, then moved book 2 back to top-level to leave the DB exactly as found.
